 fefde ke cancer ke dauraan cancer koshikaayen kis tarah sharir ke anya bhaagon main failati hai, iskaa pataa shodhakartaaon ne laga liya he
 For this, lung cancer cells first eliminate the protein, which keeps them connected to neighboring cells
 britain kii uniwarsity of manchester ke cancer research euke manchester institute kii pramukh shodhakarta angeliki maaliri ne kaha, 'is research main pehali baar yah baat saamne ai ki fefde ke cancer kii koshikaayen kis prakaar cell risical process ko kabje main kar padosi koshikaon se alag hoti hai
 The findings reveal that a protein (TIMA1) acts to interconnect cells
 jab koshikaon ke marammat kii prakriya main koi gadabadi aati he, to TIMA1 ko khatm kar us koshika ko alag kar diya jaataa he
 Healthy cells keep replacing sick cells
 lekin fefde ke cancer kii sthiti main yah prakriya aniyantrit ho jaati he, jiske parinaam swaroop TIMA1 baari paimaane par nasht hoti hai or is tarah cancer koshikaon kaa prasar hota he
 By controlling this process of recycling, lung cancer can be prevented from spreading
